m 922 285 http dbpedia resource quartet http dbpedia ontology abstract quartet four volume novel sequence written paul scott about concluding years british india series written during period ndash times called most important landmarks post fiction story quartet begins world zenith south east asia allied forces have suffered great losses burma known myanmar fallen japanese invasion indian subcontinent from east appears imminent year also marked indian nationalist leader mahatma gandhi call quit india movement british rulers india quartet this tumultuous background british soldiers civilians stationed india have duty manage this part british empire known jewel crown british monarch recurrent theme moral certainty older generation contrasted with anomie younger another shocking racism which this leads justify racism combat this danger anomie disintegration british characters themselves trapped codes principles which were part keep their fears doubts most major characters suffer difficulties some either because they follow codes which have become outmoded ahmed kasim merrick teddie bingham because they reject codes become outsiders kumar lady daphne manners sarah layton some critcs have compared quartet epic novels proust tolstoy though some critics have thought quartet straightforward example nineteenth century style realism others have argued that linear narrative style occasional outburst reams hallucinations spiritual revelations give added dimension lead characters first novel which sets stage subsequent ones daphne manners young englishwoman recently arrived india british educated indian lover hari kumar ronald merrick british police officer belonging indian police service another main character manner narration especially first volume looping elliptical shifting from back again with detours back early voices shift well perspective from third person narrative about doomed schoolteacher edwina crane first person narration another character lady chatterjee tour mayapore evening this shifting chronology while never confusing inspired much discussion http wikipedia wiki quartet
